***gesundheit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gesundheit.html>gesundheit</a> (51842)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:gesundheit.html>Gesundheit</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">health</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection_2">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gesundheit.html>gesundheit</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention"><a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>Said</a> to someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> just sneezed</span>, bless you
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2000</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:harry.html>Harry</a> Mulisch, <a href = vnd.unilang:gerrit.html>Gerrit</a> Komrij, Adriaan <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Dis, <a href = vnd.unilang:maart.html>Maarten</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>Hart</a>, Remco Campert, Marga Minco, Hugo Claus,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schrijver.html>Schrijver</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:literaire.html>literaire</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:estafette.html>estafette</a></cite>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>Bezige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>Bij</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=YYNcAAAAMAAJamp;q=%22niezen%22+%22gesundheit%22">page 142</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bleef.html>bleef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanstaren.html>aanstaren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>moest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niezen.html>niezen</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bleef.html>bleef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lachen.html>lachen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zei.html>zei</a>: '<b><a href = vnd.unilang:gesundheit.html>Gesundheit</a></b>.'</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I kept staring at her and <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> to sneeze. She kept laughing and <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>: '<b>Bless you.</b>'</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2015</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:anne.html>Anne</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tyler.html>Tyler</a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blauwe.html>blauwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:draad.html>draad</a></cite>, Prometheus, <small>→ISBN</small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=8bPHBgAAQBAJamp;pg=PT96">page 96</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">'<a href = vnd.unilang:ja.html>Ja</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:neem.html>neem</a> Heidi <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:alsjeblieft.html>alsjeblieft</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zit.html>zit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niezen.html>niezen</a>.' Heidi <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:inderdaad.html>inderdaad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niezen.html>niezen</a> – <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:serie.html>serie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zachte.html>zachte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> spetterende niesjes. '<b><a href = vnd.unilang:gesundheit.html>Gesundheit</a></b>,' <a href = vnd.unilang:zei.html>zei</a> Merrick.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">'Yes, that's alright. And take Heidi, please. She's sneezing again.' Heidi <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> sneezing indeed – a series of soft but splattering sneezes. '<b>Bless you</b>,' <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> Merrick.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2016</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:hans.html>Hans</a> Bogaert,  <cite>Echo</cite>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>Bezige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>Bij</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=yhNhDQAAQBAJamp;pg=PT60">page 60</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">'<i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gesundheit.html>Gesundheit</a></b></i>,' <a href = vnd.unilang:zei.html>zei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>moest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niezen.html>niezen</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">'<b>Bless you</b>,' he <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> as I sneezed.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>

***getogen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:getogen.html>getogen</a> (16682)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tijgen</i>. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> virtually only used in the sense of <i>raised</i> or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> up</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span>, when the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tien.html>tien</a></i> (ancestor of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tijgen</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> not yet <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> its meaning of <i>to raise</i> or <i>nurture</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:getogen.html>getogen</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> up, grown up, raised</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">getugen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gitiugon</i>. </p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to testify, bear witness, give testimony, especially in court

***getuigenis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:getuigenis.html>getuigenis</a> (5253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">getugenisse</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">getugen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bear witness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-nisse</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:getuigen.html>getuigen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nis</i>). Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zeugnis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:getuigenis.html>getuigenis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:getuigenissen.html>getuigenissen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:getuigenis.html>getuigenisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A testimony: declaration/statement serving to bear evidence or proof in an inquiry and/or trial</li>
<li>hence also other proof
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bloedig.html>Bloedige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:striemen.html>striemen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wonden.html>wonden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strekten.html>strekten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:getuigenis.html>getuigenis</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> Romeinse <a href = vnd.unilang:slaven.html>slaven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enkel.html>enkel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> foltering <b><a href = vnd.unilang:getuigenis.html>getuigenis</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:konden.html>konden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afleggen.html>afleggen</a></i>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:geval.html>geval</a></i>, from the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gevallen.html>gevallen</a></i>.

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gevancnesse</i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gēven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gevan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gebaną</i>.

***gever.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gever.html>gever</a> (20100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gevere</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>geven</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gever.html>gever</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gevers.html>gevers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gever.html>gevertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>giver, someone who gives</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a word in the dative case</li></ol>
